Kindly be informed of the new SOP concerning overstay cases with State Immigration Of Johor: 

*Students or Dependent Overstay Case Procedures*
With immediate effect, all overstay cases of students or dependents will be managed by the Enforcement Unit of Johor State Immigration, and we expect implementation of the compound.  Therefore, students must take urgent action to report to our counter for overstay cases for us to refer the matter to the immigration office.  We also strongly advise students to avoid late submissions for applications that can lead to overstay cases and result in a compound payment.

International Student & Scholar Services,
UTM International
